{"nick":"joepie91","message":"ThePendulum: \"database migration\" sounds complex, but realistically it's just this: you define \"migration files\" that do some queries, both for applying and for rollback, then when you \"run migrations\", it runs all the migration files that it hasn't run before yet, in order, and stores this \"run\" as a \"batch\". when you rollback, it just runs the \"rollback\" definition for each migration file in the last batch.","date":"2015-12-20T17:29:45.784Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"ThePendulum: that is... basically it.","date":"2015-12-20T17:29:53.267Z","type":"message"}
